welcome home
the lofts at harmony mills cohoes, ny
situated high above the scenic mohawk river, the lofts at harmony mills sets the standard for modern loft living. the building features 14-17 foot ceilings, indoor parking, fitness room, indoor pool, amenities, and soaring views unlike any in the region. eight-foot windows guarantee that your apartment will always be filled with sunshine. sleek design complements victorian architecture that made this building a national landmark.
with a professional staff and service team, all the comforts of home,  pet-friendly units, luxury services like snow and trash removal and a community of hard-working professionals who all know how to relax, the lofts at harmony mills is a secret of area locals and a respite for those fortunate enough to call this historic building home. >>click here<< schedule a tour today!

amenities
luxurious amenities at the lofts at harmony mills
you can create your own distinct lifestyle in a breathtaking setting that offers a unique combination of luxury, style and convenience. harmony mills residents are privy to some of the best and hard-to-find amenities in the area, like original hardwood flooring, smart home technology, 8ft custom windows, state of the art virtual fitness centers and an indoor pool and spa. residents enjoy stunning waterfall views, walkable downtown area and convenient location just off of highway 787 , i-90 and i-87, all within a quick 15-minute drive to downtown albany, ny.

location
lofts at harmony mills in albany, ny for rent
imagine living at the capital districts most convenient crossroad, just minutes from everything that albany, troy, and saratoga have to offer. our albany apartments are home to many who live on the river but work in albany, saratoga, clifton park, schenectady, and malta. the cohoes location is in an easy accessibility neighborhood off i-87 with access to the capital city bustle, the high-end shopping of saratoga, the one-of-a-kind shopping and movies in clifton park or the peacefulness of lake george.

privacy policy
this website uses google analytics, a web analytics service provided by google, inc. ("google"). google analytics uses cookies. the information generated by the cookie about your use of the website (including your ip address) will be transmitted to and stored by google on servers in the united states. google will use this information for the purpose of evaluating your use of the website, compiling reports on website activity for website operators and providing other services relating to website activity and internet usage. google may use the data collected to contextualize and personalize the ads of its own advertising network.  google may also transfer this information to third parties where required to do so by law, or where such third parties process the information on google's behalf. google will not associate your ip address with any other data held by google. you may refuse the use of cookies by selecting the appropriate settings on your browser, however please note that if you do this you may not be able to use the full functionality of this website. by using this website, you consent to the processing of data about you by google in the manner and for the purposes set out above. find google's privacy policy here.
